find_115(a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h) =
  if a > b
  then find_116(a,c,d,b,g,h,f)
  else find_116(b,c,d,a,g,h,e)
# n=7, i=3, c?d: a>d,a>g,b>c,b>g,c>e,d>f
find_116(a,b,c,d,e,f,g) =
  if c > d
  then find_79(a,c,e,g)
  else find_79(b,d,f,g)
# n=8, i=3, a?e: a>g,b>f,b>g,c>d,c>e,c>f,e>h
find_113(a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h) =
  if a > e
  then find_117(a,b,c,d,g,f,e)
  else find_95(d,b,e,a,h,f)
# n=7, i=3, a?b: a>e,a>g,b>e,b>f,c>d,c>f,c>g
find_117(a,b,c,d,e,f,g) =
  if a > b
  then find_118(c,a,d,b,g,e)
  else find_118(c,b,d,a,f,e)
# n=6, i=3, c?d: a>c,a>e,b>d,b>e,d>f
find_118(a,b,c,d,e,f) =
  if c > d
  then find_119(c,b,e)
  else find_79(a,d,f,e)
# n=3, i=2, a?b: b>c
find_119(a,b,c) =
  if a > b
  then b
  else find_29(a,c)
